The hot spring facilities are also very good, the environment is clean and tidy, giving people a comfortable and relaxing feeling. However, there are too many mosquitoes in the hot spring area, which affects the overall experience.
Finally, it is recommended that the hotel can open a taxi reservation service, because many five-star hotels have this service, which will further enhance the convenience and satisfaction of customers. Overall, this stay was very pleasant and we will consider visiting again.

The environment is the number one selling point of this hotel. Set amidst lush tea mountains, the hotel is surrounded by rolling hills and endless tea plantations, allowing you to enjoy the tranquility of nature.
In terms of facilities, every design of the hotel reflects the thoughtful consideration for guests. The spacious rooms were equipped with modern furniture and technology, ensuring that my stay was both comfortable and convenient. In addition, the hotel has a wide range of leisure facilities such as activity rooms and outdoor hot springs. Whether I want to maintain my daily exercise habits or simply relax, the hotel can meet my needs.
In terms of service, the hotel staff is undoubtedly its valuable asset. Not only were they professional and enthusiastic, their attention to detail was impressive. From the welcome at the front desk to the daily cleaning of the guest rooms, the service staff used their u**ost professionalism and sincerity to ensure that I was comfortable and happy throughout the journey. It is particularly worth mentioning that the hotel housekeeper Xiaoyan was able to provide personalized services according to my needs, which made me feel distinguished and extraordinary trea**ent.

Regarding dining, the hotel‚Äôs food is also a highlight. Including local specialty snacks, Huaiyang cuisine, Cantonese cuisine and other diversified menus, which can meet the needs of various tastes. Every dish not only tastes great, but also reflects a high degree of professionalism in presentation and service. The restaurant is located by the lake. Not only can you taste delicious food, but you can also enjoy koi, ducks, and black swans while enjoying the food, which adds a lot of romance.

To sum up, this resort hotel with the tea mountain as its background is extremely satisfying in terms of environment, facilities, services and catering. Not only is it an ideal place to escape the hustle and bustle of daily life and seek tranquility and relaxation, it is also an excellent choice to enjoy a high-quality life. I look forward to visiting this paradise hidden among mountains and rivers again in the near future.

Flaws that need to be pointed out:

I wanted to refund but couldn't, so I booked and refunded among many hotels. Finally, I chose Hantian for the first three days. After returning, I felt that this decision was too wise.
First of all, the service. The hotel butler called one day in advance to confirm the itinerary and added WeChat to send the location and other warm reminders. We rented a car in Hangzhou, which was about a 2-hour drive. There was a receptionist at the entrance of the lobby, who enthusiastically moved our luggage from the car to the lobby. Parking was free in the resort. After checking in, the hotel butler took us to the door of the room by parking. I booked the cliff residence on the top of the mountain. It is not a mechanical business greeting, but simple and pure, comfortable and natural. The butler sends some warm reminders on WeChat at every time period. A family letter and welcome fruit are warm and ceremonial.

Taking a bath in the bathtub in front of the window and looking at the scenery outside the window are very comfortable. In the end, I checked in and checked out at Clubmed, and I carried the suitcase myself during all the processes.

Although it is not big, the water quality is very good, which can meet the needs of children playing in the water or swimming exercise.

You can order dishes for dinner. The dishes are exquisite, the price is not too expensive, and the taste is delicious. The main dishes are tea-flavored pork knuckles, which are delicious. The average cost is about 120 yuan per person.

Mainly reflected in the following points:
1. Warm and friendly attitude, will interact with the baby, and actively ask if you need help
2. Respond and answer questions in a timely manner, and sincerely address the needs of guests. For example, we asked about the nearby mother and baby shop and she shared a small shop with affordable price not far from the hotel. The reason why I think it's affordable is because I only have one bottle of bottle cleaner and I didn't buy it, and there is a small shop a few hundred meters away that sells exactly the same thing.
3. Delicate thought for the sake of customers. For example, on the first day of our stay, we saw that we had a baby and quickly arranged a guardrail. When you see your baby being bitten by mosquitoes, offer to help provide mosquito repellents.

Because it is the first time to travel with a baby, I am a little worried, but the overall feeling is that the staff are very friendly and suitable for parent-child travel.
Baby meal: When we order beef stew, we will tell you not to add seasoning + less oil. If you change the taste, you will ask for a gnocchi soup (it seems to be called this name). There are small shrimp + mushrooms + gnocchi in it. It is very chewy, and the baby likes it very much. It is also without any condiments. It is a big bowl. If adults don't like it, it can be served with Sichuan cuisine. Boiled beef is recommended. For baby activities, there is an indoor and an outdoor children's playground, and there are peacocks + pheasants outdoors. You can go to hot springs and swimming pools. There is also a Sixiantang next to the restaurant with children's books + chess and cards and other facilities.

In addition to Xiaojuan, I would also like to commend Guan Xiujuan. She is a staff member in the women's changing room in the hot spring. Seeing that I was in a hurry with my baby, she took the initiative to help protect the baby. She also told me to take a dry bath towel to avoid The baby is cold. Later, when I came out, I saw that the baby was bitten by mosquitoes and put mosquito repellent stickers on us and warmly greeted us to come back the next day. I was very moved, so I quickly looked at her badge and wrote down her name, but I was a little unsure if I remembered it accurately because I was busy with the baby, but I still wanted to express my gratitude. There is also a little girl in the restaurant. She has never had a badge and I don't know her name, but she can be seen every morning and evening at dinner, mainly in the middle and rear areas, and she looks young. We lost a bowl on the first day of eating and she helped us collect it and return it to us. During breakfast, she would walk around with a drink cart, and when I needed coffee, she would happily tell me how she researched how to make coffee better. I drank it and it tasted better than coffee I remember, not so bitter. These little bit of kind and friendly details add up to an overall great experience.

Finally, some suggestions: bring the children back from the outside at night and call a shuttle bus at the front desk to go to Yaju. Because the children were a little tired all day, we kept standing outside waiting for the bus. Taking the shuttle bus is also very fast in our experience, and many times there are no people. As a result, the car just arrived, and the uncle at the door was helping another car park, so he didn't pay attention. Suddenly rushing out from the lobby, seven or eight people, old and young, all dressed in nightgowns, rushed directly into the car and sat down. Because I didn't rob them with my child, I had to go to the front desk to call for another one. The overall reason is mainly this group of unqualified people, but I also want to give a suggestion to the hotel, whether it is possible to pull a guardrail at the entrance of the lobby when there are many people, so that at least order can be achieved, first-come-last-arrival, rather than obeying Rules for guests to be patient. The front desk of the hotel and the housekeeper Xiaojuan expressed their apologies and made suggestions here, hoping to improve in this regard. In addition, if you live in a cliff dwelling, you can see insects every day. If you mind, it may be better to recommend the mountain.
